Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}
Note: normalizeFlag mutates state.issues — needs state import if extracted.Lines 209-231: Data loadingasync function loadData() {
  const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}
Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/display.jsfunction setMeta(title, trail) {
  pageTitle.textContent = title;
  breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
    a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
  });
}

function badge(status) {
  return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
}

function chip(label, value) {
  return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
}

function displayFlag(value) {
  return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayConfidence(value) {
  return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayLevel(value) {
  return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayPrice(value) {
  return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
  return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
}

Dependencies: state (state.js), uniq (utils.js), avgRating (line 944), statCount (line 929).Lines 448-468: Routing helpers — parseHashRoute, queueViewStatefunction parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
}

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}
Lines ~1760-1810: Agent draft storage keys cluster (storage location #1) Functions: editorialDraftEntries, patchConsoleEntries, importConsoleEntries, agentDraftStorageKey, verificationDraftStorageKey, agentDraftEntries, verificationDraftEntries, agentRunHistoryStorageKey, agentRunHistoryEntries, savedAgentBatchStorageKey, savedAgentBatchEntries. All depend on getStoredList.Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2) Three core storage primitives:function getStoredList(key) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}
Note: normalizeFlag mutates state.issues — needs state import if extracted.Lines 209-231: Data loadingasync function loadData() {
  const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}
Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/display.jsfunction setMeta(title, trail) {
  pageTitle.textContent = title;
  breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
    a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
  });
}

function badge(status) {
  return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
}

function chip(label, value) {
  return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
}

function displayFlag(value) {
  return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayConfidence(value) {
  return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayLevel(value) {
  return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayPrice(value) {
  return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
  return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
}

Dependencies: state (state.js), uniq (utils.js), avgRating (line 944), statCount (line 929).Lines 448-468: Routing helpers — parseHashRoute, queueViewStatefunction parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
}

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

All depend on getStoredList.Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2) Three core storage primitives:function getStoredList(key) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}
Note: normalizeFlag mutates state.issues — needs state import if extracted.Lines 209-231: Data loadingasync function loadData() {
  const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}
Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/display.jsfunction setMeta(title, trail) {
  pageTitle.textContent = title;
  breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
    a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
  });
}

function badge(status) {
  return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
}

function chip(label, value) {
  return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
}

function displayFlag(value) {
  return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayConfidence(value) {
  return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayLevel(value) {
  return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayPrice(value) {
  return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
  return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
}
Note: setMeta references DOM globals pageTitle and breadcrumbs — stays in main or needs DOM refs passed. badge depends on esc (utils) and STATUS_AR (constants). displayFlag depends on FLAG_AR, etc.Lines 269-446: Analytics queries — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/analytics.js Full functions read: topRatedRecords, topDistrictGroups, sourceVerificationState, districtVerificationState, confidenceVerificationState, verificationQueues, featuredStatuses, importantMissingFields, recordsMissingImportant, lowConfidenceRecords, recentVerifiedRecords, newlyAddedRecords, todayVerifiedCount, queueHref, entityHref. Dependencies: state (state.js), uniq (utils.js), avgRating (line 944), statCount (line 929).Lines 448-468: Routing helpers — parseHashRoute, queueViewStatefunction parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
}

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}
Lines ~1760-1810: Agent draft storage keys cluster (storage location #1) Functions: editorialDraftEntries, patchConsoleEntries, importConsoleEntries, agentDraftStorageKey, verificationDraftStorageKey, agentDraftEntries, verificationDraftEntries, agentRunHistoryStorageKey, agentRunHistoryEntries, savedAgentBatchStorageKey, savedAgentBatchEntries. All depend on getStoredList.Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2) Three core storage primitives:function getStoredList(key) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}
Also: reviewSessionStorageKey, exportHistoryStorageKey, editorialDraftsStorageKey, patchConsoleStorageKey, importConsoleStorageKey, evidenceLabStorageKey, verificationSessionStorageKey, verificationDecisionStorageKey, missionRegistryStorageKey, missionSessionStorageKey, getExportHistory, saveExportHistory.Lines NOT read verbatim but known from function inventory:

Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}
Note: normalizeFlag mutates state.issues — needs state import if extracted.Lines 209-231: Data loadingasync function loadData() {
  const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}
Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/display.jsfunction setMeta(title, trail) {
  pageTitle.textContent = title;
  breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;

    a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
  });
}

function badge(status) {
  return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
}

function chip(label, value) {
  return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
}

function displayFlag(value) {
  return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayConfidence(value) {
  return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayLevel(value) {
  return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayPrice(value) {
  return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
  return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
}

Dependencies: state (state.js), uniq (utils.js), avgRating (line 944), statCount (line 929).Lines 448-468: Routing helpers — parseHashRoute, queueViewStatefunction parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
}

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

All depend on getStoredList.Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2) Three core storage primitives:function getStoredList(key) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}
Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/display.jsfunction setMeta(title, trail) {
  pageTitle.textContent = title;
  breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
    a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
  });
}

function badge(status) {
  return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
}

function chip(label, value) {
  return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
}

function displayFlag(value) {
  return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayConfidence(value) {
  return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
}

function displayLevel(value) {
  return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayPrice(value) {
  return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
}

function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
  return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
}

Dependencies: state (state.js), uniq (utils.js), avgRating (line 944), statCount (line 929).Lines 448-468: Routing helpers — parseHashRoute, queueViewStatefunction parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
}

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

All depend on getStoredList.Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2) Three core storage primitives:function getStoredList(key) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

  }

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

 function esc(v = '') {
   return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
 }

 function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
 ```

 **Lines 181-207: Data normalization — `normalizeFlag` and `normalizeRecord`**
 ```javascript
 function normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
   const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
   if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
   if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
   if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
   if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
   state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
   return 'unknown';
 }

 function normalizeRecord(record) {
   const normalized = {
     ...record,
     _norm: {
       work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
       group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
       late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
       specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
       desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
       family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
       indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
       outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
       parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
     }
   };
   return normalized;
 }
 ```
 Note: `normalizeFlag` mutates `state.issues` — needs state import if extracted.

 async function loadData() {
   const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
   if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
   state.raw = await res.json();
   const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
   state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
 }

 async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
   try {
     const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
     if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
     state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
   } catch (error) {
     state.agentRuntime = {
       ok: false,
       available: false,
       mode: 'unavailable',
       label: 'غير متاح',
       note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
     };

 }

 function setMeta(title, trail) {
   pageTitle.textContent = title;
   breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
   document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
     a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
   });

 }

 function chip(label, value) {
   return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
 }

 function displayFlag(value) {
   return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
 }

 function displayConfidence(value) {
   return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
 }

 function displayLevel(value) {
   return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
 }

 function displayPrice(value) {
   return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
 }

 function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
   return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
 }

 ```javascript
 function parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
   const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
   const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
   const parts = pathPart.split('/');
   return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
 }
 ```

     function esc(v = '') {
       return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
     }

     function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }

     **Lines 181-207: Data normalization — `normalizeFlag` and `normalizeRecord`**
     ```javascript
     function normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
       const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
       if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
       if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
       if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
       if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
       state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
       return 'unknown';
     }

     function normalizeRecord(record) {
       const normalized = {
         ...record,
         _norm: {
           work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
           group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
           late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
           specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
           desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
           family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
           indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
           outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
           parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
         }
       };
       return normalized;
     }
     ```
     Note: `normalizeFlag` mutates `state.issues` — needs state import if extracted.

     **Lines 209-231: Data loading**
     ```javascript
     async function loadData() {
       const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
       if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
       state.raw = await res.json();
       const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
       state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
     }

     async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
       try {
         const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
         if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
         state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
       } catch (error) {
         state.agentRuntime = {
           ok: false,
           available: false,
           mode: 'unavailable',
           label: 'غير متاح',
           note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
         };
       }
     }
     ```

     **Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for `modules/display.js`**
     ```javascript
     function setMeta(title, trail) {
       pageTitle.textContent = title;
       breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
       document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
         a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
       });
     }

     function badge(status) {
       return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
     }

     function chip(label, value) {
       return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
     }

     function displayFlag(value) {
       return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayConfidence(value) {
       return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayLevel(value) {
       return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayPrice(value) {
       return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
       return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
     }
     ```

     ```javascript
     function parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
       const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
       const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
       const parts = pathPart.split('/');
       return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
     }
     ```

     **Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analytics**
     ```javascript
     function statCount(status) {
       return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
     }

     function currentSector() {
       return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
     }

     function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
       const entry = sectorTree()
         .flatMap(group => group.children)
         .find(child => child.key === key);
       return entry?.title || key;
     }

     function avgRating(records) {
       const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
       if (!nums.length) return '—';
       return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
     }

     function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
       return records.filter(r => {
         if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
         if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
         if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
         if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
         if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
         if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
         if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
         if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
         return true;
       });
     }
     ```

     **Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2)**
     Three core storage primitives:
     ```javascript
     function getStoredList(key) {
       try {
         const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
         return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
       } catch {
         return [];
       }
     }

     function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
       localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
     }

     function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
       const list = getStoredList(key);
       const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
       if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
       else list.unshift(item);
       saveStoredList(key, list);
     }
     ```
     Also: `reviewSessionStorageKey`, `exportHistoryStorageKey`, `editorialDraftsStorageKey`, `patchConsoleStorageKey`, `importConsoleStorageKey`, `evidenceLabStorageKey`, `verificationSessionStorageKey`, `verificationDecisionStorageKey`, `missionRegistryStorageKey`, `missionSessionStorageKey`, `getExportHistory`, `saveExportHistory`.

     function esc(v = '') {
       return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
     }

     function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
     ```

     **Lines 181-207: Data normalization — `normalizeFlag` and `normalizeRecord`**
     ```javascript
     function normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
       const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
       if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
       if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
       if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
       if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
       state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
       return 'unknown';
     }

     function normalizeRecord(record) {
       const normalized = {
         ...record,
         _norm: {
           work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
           group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
           late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
           specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
           desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
           family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
           indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
           outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
           parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
         }
       };
       return normalized;
     }
     ```
     Note: `normalizeFlag` mutates `state.issues` — needs state import if extracted.

     **Lines 209-231: Data loading**
     ```javascript
     async function loadData() {
       const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
       if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
       state.raw = await res.json();
       const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
       state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
     }

     async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
       try {
         const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
         if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
         state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
       } catch (error) {
         state.agentRuntime = {
           ok: false,
           available: false,
           mode: 'unavailable',
           label: 'غير متاح',
           note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
         };
       }
     }
     ```

     **Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for `modules/display.js`**
     ```javascript
     function setMeta(title, trail) {
       pageTitle.textContent = title;
       breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
       document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
         a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
       });
     }

     function badge(status) {
       return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
     }

     function chip(label, value) {
       return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
     }

     function displayFlag(value) {
       return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayConfidence(value) {
       return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayLevel(value) {
       return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayPrice(value) {
       return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
       return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
     }
     ```
     Note: `setMeta` references DOM globals `pageTitle` and `breadcrumbs` — stays in main or needs DOM refs passed. `badge` depends on `esc` (utils) and `STATUS_AR` (constants). `displayFlag` depends on `FLAG_AR`, etc.

     ```javascript
     function parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
       const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
       const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
       const parts = pathPart.split('/');
       return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
     }
     ```

     **Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analytics**
     ```javascript
     function statCount(status) {
       return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
     }

     function currentSector() {
       return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
     }

     function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
       const entry = sectorTree()
         .flatMap(group => group.children)
         .find(child => child.key === key);
       return entry?.title || key;
     }

     function avgRating(records) {
       const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
       if (!nums.length) return '—';
       return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
     }

     function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
       return records.filter(r => {
         if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
         if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
         if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
         if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
         if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
         if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
         if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
         if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
         return true;
       });
     }
     ```

     **Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2)**
     Three core storage primitives:
     ```javascript
     function getStoredList(key) {
       try {
         const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
         return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
       } catch {
         return [];
       }
     }

     function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
       localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
     }

     function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
       const list = getStoredList(key);
       const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
       if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
       else list.unshift(item);
       saveStoredList(key, list);
     }
     ```
     Also: `reviewSessionStorageKey`, `exportHistoryStorageKey`, `editorialDraftsStorageKey`, `patchConsoleStorageKey`, `importConsoleStorageKey`, `evidenceLabStorageKey`, `verificationSessionStorageKey`, `verificationDecisionStorageKey`, `missionRegistryStorageKey`, `missionSessionStorageKey`, `getExportHistory`, `saveExportHistory`.

       return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
     }

     function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
     ```

     **Lines 181-207: Data normalization — `normalizeFlag` and `normalizeRecord`**
     ```javascript
     function normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
       const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
       if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
       if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
       if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
       if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
       state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
       return 'unknown';
     }

     function normalizeRecord(record) {
       const normalized = {
         ...record,
         _norm: {
           work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
           group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
           late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
           specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
           desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
           family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
           indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
           outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
           parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
         }
       };
       return normalized;
     }
     ```
     Note: `normalizeFlag` mutates `state.issues` — needs state import if extracted.

     **Lines 209-231: Data loading**
     ```javascript
     async function loadData() {
       const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
       if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
       state.raw = await res.json();
       const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
       state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
     }

     async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
       try {
         const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
         if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
         state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
       } catch (error) {
         state.agentRuntime = {
           ok: false,
           available: false,
           mode: 'unavailable',
           label: 'غير متاح',
           note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
         };
       }
     }
     ```

     **Lines 233-267: Display helpers — EXTRACTION TARGET for `modules/display.js`**
     ```javascript
     function setMeta(title, trail) {
       pageTitle.textContent = title;
       breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
       document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
         a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
       });
     }

     function badge(status) {
       return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
     }

     function chip(label, value) {
       return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
     }

     function displayFlag(value) {
       return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayConfidence(value) {
       return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayLevel(value) {
       return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayPrice(value) {
       return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
       return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
     }
     ```
     Note: `setMeta` references DOM globals `pageTitle` and `breadcrumbs` — stays in main or needs DOM refs passed. `badge` depends on `esc` (utils) and `STATUS_AR` (constants). `displayFlag` depends on `FLAG_AR`, etc.

     **Lines 448-468: Routing helpers — `parseHashRoute`, `queueViewState`**
     ```javascript
     function parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
       const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
       const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
       const parts = pathPart.split('/');
       return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
     }
     ```

     **Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analytics**
     ```javascript
     function statCount(status) {
       return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
     }

     function currentSector() {
       return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
     }

     function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
       const entry = sectorTree()
         .flatMap(group => group.children)
         .find(child => child.key === key);
       return entry?.title || key;
     }

     function avgRating(records) {
       const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
       if (!nums.length) return '—';
       return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
     }

     function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
       return records.filter(r => {
         if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
         if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
         if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
         if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
         if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
         if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
         if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
         if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
         return true;
       });
     }
     ```

     **Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2)**
     Three core storage primitives:
     ```javascript
     function getStoredList(key) {
       try {
         const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
         return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
       } catch {
         return [];
       }
     }

     function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
       localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
     }

     function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
       const list = getStoredList(key);
       const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
       if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
       else list.unshift(item);
       saveStoredList(key, list);
     }
     ```
     Also: `reviewSessionStorageKey`, `exportHistoryStorageKey`, `editorialDraftsStorageKey`, `patchConsoleStorageKey`, `importConsoleStorageKey`, `evidenceLabStorageKey`, `verificationSessionStorageKey`, `verificationDecisionStorageKey`, `missionRegistryStorageKey`, `missionSessionStorageKey`, `getExportHistory`, `saveExportHistory`.

Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}

  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}

  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}

    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

All depend on getStoredList.Lines ~4461-4545: Storage key functions + core storage utilities (storage location #2) Three core storage primitives:function getStoredList(key) {
  try {
    const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
    return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
}

function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
}

function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
  const list = getStoredList(key);
  const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
  if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
  else list.unshift(item);
  saveStoredList(key, list);
}

Lines 175-179: Utility functions — EXTRACTION TARGET for modules/utils.jsfunction esc(v = '') {
  return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
}

function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
Lines 181-207: Data normalization — normalizeFlag and normalizeRecordfunction normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
  const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
  if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
  if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
  if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
  state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
  return 'unknown';
}

function normalizeRecord(record) {
  const normalized = {
    ...record,
    _norm: {
      work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
      group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
      late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
      specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
      desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
      family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
      indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
      outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
      parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
    }
  };
  return normalized;
}
Note: normalizeFlag mutates state.issues — needs state import if extracted.Lines 209-231: Data loadingasync function loadData() {
  const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
  state.raw = await res.json();
  const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
  state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
}

async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
  try {
    const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
    state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
  } catch (error) {
    state.agentRuntime = {
      ok: false,
      available: false,
      mode: 'unavailable',
      label: 'غير متاح',
      note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
    };
  }
}

}

}

  const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
  const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
  const parts = pathPart.split('/');
  return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
}
Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analyticsfunction statCount(status) {
  return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
}

function currentSector() {
  return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
}

function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
  const entry = sectorTree()
    .flatMap(group => group.children)
    .find(child => child.key === key);
  return entry?.title || key;
}

function avgRating(records) {
  const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
  if (!nums.length) return '—';
  return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
}

function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
  return records.filter(r => {
    if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
    if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
    if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
    if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
    if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
    if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
    if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
    if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

1. Primary Request and Intent:

   **First request (COMPLETED):** "اطلع على المشروع ثم اخبرني رايك كمختص وتقني متخصص" — Review the entire project and provide an expert technical opinion. This was delivered as a comprehensive Arabic technical review covering architecture, server, database, frontend, agent system, and documentation.

   **Second request (ONGOING — the critical operational mandate):** The user provided extremely detailed operational requirements for a **systematic modular refactor** of the project "دليل بريدة الشامل" (Daleely Buraidah Wiki). Key aspects:

   - **Paradigm shift:** treat the project as an **internal operating system**, not just a SPA
   - Focus on **maintainability and systematic development**, not impressions
   - **Five identified deficiencies:** monolithic script.js, monolithic styles.css, missing documentation, no architectural boundaries, need for systematic refactor

   **Explicit constraints (CRITICAL — must be preserved):**
   - NO framework migration
   - NO SQLite migration
   - NO full rebuild from scratch
   - NO changes to master.json or data pipeline
   - NO cosmetic improvements that don't serve maintainability
   - SAFE refactor preserving current behavior

   **4 Phases ordered:**
   1. Architecture Clarification (map current layers, target module map, split priorities)
   2. Safe Modular Refactor (first batch of highest-value splits from script.js)
   3. Documentation System (README, architecture docs, flow docs, sector expansion guide)
   4. Stabilization After Refactor (test paths, fix breakage, unify naming)

   **Immediate execution request:** Start Phase 1 and 2 simultaneously — architecture map THEN immediately begin actual refactoring. User's exact words: "أريدك الآن أن تبدأ مباشرة بالمرحلة الأولى والثانية معًا" and "لا تتوقف عند التخطيط فقط" (Don't stop at planning only).

   **Priority order:** maintainability > modular clarity > safe refactor > behavior preservation

   5. What remains in the monolith

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - Node.js ESM server (`node:http` native, zero dependencies, `"type": "module"` in package.json)
   - SPA with hash-based routing (`window.addEventListener('hashchange', router)`)
   - Central mutable state object (`const state = {...}`) referenced 211 times across script.js
   - Agent-based AI runtime: Record Completion Agent + Verification Support Agent
   - Runtime proxy pattern: external HTTP runtime with mock fallback
   - Field-level whitelisting for security (ALLOWED_COMPLETION_FIELDS, ALLOWED_VERIFICATION_FIELDS)
   - Draft-only mode enforcement (no direct data writes)
   - localStorage-based state persistence (7 references) for sessions, decisions, drafts, evidence
   - Arabic RTL (`dir="rtl"`) with dark theme using CSS custom properties
   - Monolithic frontend: 8,665 lines, 321 top-level functions, ~25 routes
   - ESM modules already enabled in package.json — ready for modular splitting
   - `script.js` loaded via `<script src="script.js?v=20260313-1"></script>` (NOT as module yet — needs `type="module"` to enable ESM imports)
   - Batch processing for agents (up to 120 items)
   - Audit trail with sequential write queue on server
   - Verification workflow with source, district, and confidence state machines
   - Mission system for structured data improvement campaigns
   - Release/patch pipeline with readiness scoring, signoff, and export
   - Storage functions scattered across multiple non-contiguous locations in script.js (lines ~1760-1810 AND ~4461-4540)
   - Three core storage primitives: `getStoredList`, `saveStoredList`, `upsertStoredItem`

     **Lines 181-207: Data normalization — `normalizeFlag` and `normalizeRecord`**
     ```javascript
     function normalizeFlag(value, fieldName = '') {
       const raw = String(value ?? '').trim().toLowerCase();
       if (!raw || raw === 'unknown') return 'unknown';
       if (['yes', 'true'].includes(raw)) return 'yes';
       if (['no', 'false'].includes(raw)) return 'no';
       if (['partial', 'mixed'].includes(raw)) return 'partial';
       state.issues.push(`normalize:${fieldName}:${value}`);
       return 'unknown';
     }

     function normalizeRecord(record) {
       const normalized = {
         ...record,
         _norm: {
           work_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.work_friendly, 'work_friendly'),
           group_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.group_friendly, 'group_friendly'),
           late_night: normalizeFlag(record.late_night, 'late_night'),
           specialty_coffee: normalizeFlag(record.specialty_coffee, 'specialty_coffee'),
           desserts: normalizeFlag(record.desserts, 'desserts'),
           family_friendly: normalizeFlag(record.family_friendly, 'family_friendly'),
           indoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.indoor_seating, 'indoor_seating'),
           outdoor_seating: normalizeFlag(record.outdoor_seating, 'outdoor_seating'),
           parking: normalizeFlag(record.parking, 'parking'),
         }
       };
       return normalized;
     }
     ```
     Note: `normalizeFlag` mutates `state.issues` — needs state import if extracted.

     **Lines 209-231: Data loading**
     ```javascript
     async function loadData() {
       const res = await fetch(DATA_URL, { cache: 'no-store' });
       if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load ${DATA_URL}`);
       state.raw = await res.json();
       const records = Array.isArray(state.raw.records) ? state.raw.records : [];
       state.records = records.map(normalizeRecord);
     }

     async function refreshAgentRuntimeInfo() {
       try {
         const res = await fetch('./api/runtime/health', { cache: 'no-store' });
         if (!res.ok) throw new Error('runtime unavailable');
         state.agentRuntime = await res.json();
       } catch (error) {
         state.agentRuntime = {
           ok: false,
           available: false,
           mode: 'unavailable',
           label: 'غير متاح',
           note: 'لا يوجد proxy runtime نشط حاليًا، وسيبقى الوكيل على الوضع المحلي فقط.',
         };
       }
     }

     ```javascript
     function setMeta(title, trail) {
       pageTitle.textContent = title;
       breadcrumbs.textContent = trail;
       document.querySelectorAll('.nav-group a').forEach(a => {
         a.classList.toggle('active', location.hash.startsWith(a.getAttribute('href')));
       });
     }

     function badge(status) {
       return `<span class="badge ${esc(status)}">${esc(STATUS_AR[status] || status)}</span>`;
     }

     function chip(label, value) {
       return `<span class="chip"><strong>${esc(label)}:</strong> ${esc(value)}</span>`;
     }

     function displayFlag(value) {
       return FLAG_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayConfidence(value) {
       return CONFIDENCE_AR[value] || value || '—';
     }

     function displayLevel(value) {
       return LEVEL_AR[String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayPrice(value) {
       return PRICE_AR[String(value || '').trim()] || value || 'غير متحقق';
     }

     function displayText(value, fallback = 'غير متحقق') {
       return String(value || '').trim() || fallback;
     }
     ```

     function parseHashRoute(hash = location.hash || '#/dashboard') {
       const cleaned = hash.replace(/^#\//, '');
       const [pathPart, queryPart = ''] = cleaned.split('?');
       const parts = pathPart.split('/');
       return { parts, query: new URLSearchParams(queryPart) };
     }
     ```

     **Lines 929-962: Helper functions needed by analytics**
     ```javascript
     function statCount(status) {
       return state.records.filter(r => r.status === status).length;
     }

     function currentSector() {
       return uniq(state.records.map(r => r.sector).filter(Boolean));
     }

     function sectorLabelByKey(key = '') {
       const entry = sectorTree()
         .flatMap(group => group.children)
         .find(child => child.key === key);
       return entry?.title || key;
     }

     function avgRating(records) {
       const nums = records.map(r => Number(r.google_rating)).filter(n => !Number.isNaN(n));
       if (!nums.length) return '—';
       return (nums.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / nums.length).toFixed(2);
     }

     function filterRecords(records = state.records) {
       return records.filter(r => {
         if (state.filters.status && r.status !== state.filters.status) return false;
         if (state.filters.district && r.district !== state.filters.district) return false;
         if (state.filters.confidence && r.confidence !== state.filters.confidence) return false;
         if (state.filters.specialty && r._norm.specialty_coffee !== state.filters.specialty) return false;
         if (state.filters.desserts && r._norm.desserts !== state.filters.desserts) return false;
         if (state.filters.work && r._norm.work_friendly !== state.filters.work) return false;
         if (state.filters.groups && r._norm.group_friendly !== state.filters.groups) return false;
         if (state.filters.late && r._norm.late_night !== state.filters.late) return false;
         return true;
       });
     }
     ```

     Three core storage primitives:
     ```javascript
     function getStoredList(key) {
       try {
         const raw = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '[]');
         return Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : [];
       } catch {
         return [];
       }
     }

     function saveStoredList(key, items = []) {
       localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items.slice(0, 40)));
     }

     function upsertStoredItem(key, item, idField = 'id') {
       const list = getStoredList(key);
       const index = list.findIndex(entry => entry[idField] === item[idField]);
       if (index >= 0) list[index] = { ...list[index], ...item };
       else list.unshift(item);
       saveStoredList(key, list);
     }
     ```
     Also: `reviewSessionStorageKey`, `exportHistoryStorageKey`, `editorialDraftsStorageKey`, `patchConsoleStorageKey`, `importConsoleStorageKey`, `evidenceLabStorageKey`, `verificationSessionStorageKey`, `verificationDecisionStorageKey`, `missionRegistryStorageKey`, `missionSessionStorageKey`, `getExportHistory`, `saveExportHistory`.

     function esc(v = '') {
       return String(v).replace(/[&<>"']/g, m => ({ '&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;' }[m]));
     }

     function uniq(arr) { return [...new Set(arr)]; }
